We asked whether PI3K induction, triggered by TCR activation, could influence Hes-1 levels (Fig. 2A). Significantly, this induction was also blocked by the gamma secretase inhibitor DAPT, consistent with an absolute requirement for N-IC.">

We asked whether PI3K induction, triggered by TCR activation, could influence Hes-1 levels (Fig. 2A). In the absence of any exogenously added Delta 1 (open bars-IgG control), TCR activation (with anti-CD3/anti-CD28 antibodies) up-regulated Hes-1 levels in a LY294002-sensitive manner. Significantly, this induction was also blocked by the gamma secretase inhibitor DAPT, consistent with an absolute requirement for N-IC.
